  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_623dc1df-7ef7-4932-b44d-393437afd8ee'
      });

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer15763155220699479722">Sarai was only fourteen when her mother uprooted her to live in Mexico with a notorious drug lord. Over time she forgot what it was like to live a normal life, but she never let go of her hope to escape the compound where she has been held for the past nine years.<br/><br/>Victor is a cold-blooded assassin who, like Sarai, has known only death and violence since he was a young boy. </span>
  <span id="freeText15763155220699479722" style="display:none">Sarai was only fourteen when her mother uprooted her to live in Mexico with a notorious drug lord. Over time she forgot what it was like to live a normal life, but she never let go of her hope to escape the compound where she has been held for the past nine years.<br /><br />Victor is a cold-blooded assassin who, like Sarai, has known only death and violence since he was a young boy. When Victor arrives at the compound to collect details and payment for a hit, Sarai sees him as her only opportunity for escape. But things don’t go as planned and instead of finding transport back to Tucson, she finds herself free from one dangerous man and caught in the clutches of another.<br /><br />While on the run, Victor strays from his primal nature as he succumbs to his conscience and resolves to help Sarai. As they grow closer, he finds himself willing to risk everything to keep her alive; even his relationship with his devoted brother and liaison, Niklas, who now like everyone else wants Sarai dead.<br /><br />As Victor and Sarai slowly build a trust, the differences between them seem to lessen, and an unlikely attraction intensifies. But Victor’s brutal skills and experience may not be enough in the end to save her, as the power she unknowingly holds over him may ultimately be what gets her killed.<br /><br />This is their story…</span>
  <a data-text-id="15763155220699479722" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_646127655" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646127655" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646127655?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=suspenseful">suspenseful</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=dark">dark</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646127655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8885185245495707345"><b>*4.5 Stars*</b><br/><br/><b>Now <i>THAT</i> is how to make readers fearlessly fall for the bad-boy!</b><br/><br/><i>Killing Sarai</i> is an action-packed, unconventional love story that will undoubtably push your boundaries as a reader. Its bold setting takes place in a twisted world where kidnapping, sex slavery, and cold-blooded murder barely induce so much as a flinch. Its intensity will astound you and its unique character development will have you unashamedly rooting for the bad-guy—who, quite possibly, is not as bad as he seems...<br/><br/><b>Sar</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8885185245495707345" style="display:none"><b>*4.5 Stars*</b><br><br><b>Now <i>THAT</i> is how to make readers fearlessly fall for the bad-boy!</b><br><br><i>Killing Sarai</i> is an action-packed, unconventional love story that will undoubtably push your boundaries as a reader. Its bold setting takes place in a twisted world where kidnapping, sex slavery, and cold-blooded murder barely induce so much as a flinch. Its intensity will astound you and its unique character development will have you unashamedly rooting for the bad-guy—who, quite possibly, is not as bad as he seems...<br><br><b>Sarai</b> has been living in seclusion for years. Kidnapped at the tender age of fourteen and forced to witness rape, abuse, and murder, she has successfully grown numb to the effects of all things grotesque. Sarai, although also abused, remains her captor's <i>favorite</i>—oddly obtaining a sort of twisted <b>'princess'</b> status amongst the slaves. When she finally garners enough courage to run, it is straight into the frigid arms of a cold-blooded hit man...<br><br><b>Victor</b> lives for one thing: <b>murder for money.</b> He's cold, calculated and precise—but he does display a conscience. He exudes a sexy confidence and has no room in his 'killing' schedule for a <i>relationship</i>, of any sort. Sarai is a distraction, as well as a threat. He'll use her presence only to gain the upper hand, and then she's a goner. <br><br>He <b>can't</b> feel for her.<br>He <b>won't</b> fall for her.<br>But this may be the one thing over which the competent Victor has no control...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"What have you done to me?" He says.<br>"I was going to ask you the same question."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The way these horrific events unfold is ingenious. The author uses such an eloquent demeanor in delivering these blows; it almost feels like a contradiction. This is not a pretty love story by any means, but its execution is beautiful. <br><br>This story is told through dual perspectives. To be honest, I've become a bit wary of dual POV's; sometimes I enjoy deciphering a character's thoughts solely through their actions. I also find that some heroes lose their edge once the perspectives switch. But this author handled the transition seamlessly, and successfully added more vigor into an already intense story. Victor retained the same mystery and allure when revealed to us through his own perspective, and I appreciated the consistency. <br><br>The final 30% of this book truly took my breath away. It took an unexpected turn, slightly twisting the tone into something darker, and it is precisely what made this a five-star read for me. The ending is not complete, although there is enough finality to keep you from pulling your hair out. That said, the open ending suggests a <i>killer</i> follow-up, and I honestly cannot wait! <b>AMAZING read!</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Romance/Dark <br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Mild amount/Maximum Steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Unconventional, complicated, intense. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Sexy, bad-boy killer with a conscience. Damaged but willful heroine. Brilliantly portrayed. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Centered on an untraditional relationship formed within an intense and sinister lifestyle. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Experienced and captivating. Well-planned out execution. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Dual perspectives<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> Mild/doable. Sets stage for more story. <br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Follow up<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_639236769" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639236769" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639236769?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639236769" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4736120060666683256"><b>5 MUST READ STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/9b53a4ac-7567-42bc-a425-bc11a7b406ea_zpse12ce9d3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425059i/847835._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 9b53a4ac-7567-42bc-a425-bc11a7b406ea_zpse12ce9d3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Wow... just wow. That is the first thing that comes to mind when I think about this book. It really ‘wowed’ me. J.A. Redmerski just has a knack for writing my favorite books. This book is so different from the Edge of Never, but just as good. Darker reads, books with a little bit of a twist. Books where the hero is really the ‘bad guy’ too. Those are my absolute favorites. And this book fit right into that category. <br/><br/><br/>Sarai is a girl who has been a prisoner of a Mexican dru</span>
  <span id="freeText4736120060666683256" style="display:none"><b>5 MUST READ STARS!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/9b53a4ac-7567-42bc-a425-bc11a7b406ea_zpse12ce9d3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425059i/847835._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9b53a4ac-7567-42bc-a425-bc11a7b406ea_zpse12ce9d3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Wow... just wow. That is the first thing that comes to mind when I think about this book. It really ‘wowed’ me. J.A. Redmerski just has a knack for writing my favorite books. This book is so different from the Edge of Never, but just as good. Darker reads, books with a little bit of a twist. Books where the hero is really the ‘bad guy’ too. Those are my absolute favorites. And this book fit right into that category. <br><br><br>Sarai is a girl who has been a prisoner of a Mexican drug lord since she has been fourteen. For nine years. She wasn’t kidnapped, she was handed off by her own mother. Now she is stuck there, with no means to escape. Until one night, she hears him. Victor. Victor is an American. He is hired by Javier (drug lord) to kill a man. Thats his job. Victor is a cold blooded killer. He doesn’t kill ‘innocents’ but he has been killing for a long time. He doesn’t have sympathy for anyone or remorse for what he does. Its what he was born to do, what he was trained to do. What he’s been doing for as long as he can remember.<br><br>When Sarai sees this American, she thinks... this is my one shot to get out of here. She takes it. She runs and sneaks into Victor’s car. This is the start of Sarai and Victor’s journey together. Victor isn’t there to help Sarai, but he keeps her around for a bit because he knows she will be useful. She is a ‘prize’ for Javier, his favorite girl, and he knows he can bargain with her. Sarai isn’t going back. One way or another, her time with Javier is over. If she ever faces him again one of two things will happen. She will kill him, or she will die trying. Either way, she’s not living that life again. Even though Victor is a killer, she knows he is, she feels safe with him. Maybe not at first, but she grows to want him around, need him around. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Despite my growing fear, I still want to be right where I am, trapped in the merciless arms of a killer.”</blockquote>
</i><br>This story was surprising, unpredictable. I found myself unable to put it down, just thinking... what is going to happen next??? <b>Victor</b>. Victor is ‘the bad guy’, but not really. Getting deeper into his character, we see why Victor has the cold exterior he has, why he is the way he is. He is something else.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/c7add377-c0bc-41a9-8c4f-9f273637901b_zps0aee17e1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425059i/847836.jpg" alt=" photo c7add377-c0bc-41a9-8c4f-9f273637901b_zps0aee17e1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Victor has been doing his job a long time. He never screws up. Ever. If he did, it would mean death. He follows orders, follows the rules. No exceptions. But there is something about this girl, about Sarai that is different. He doesn’t know why, but he needs to help her, to protect her. It’s a dangerous game they are playing. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/63ad1e15-91c5-4d6f-b7ad-199d862d15d4_zpse92cd7f4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425059i/847837.jpg" alt=" photo 63ad1e15-91c5-4d6f-b7ad-199d862d15d4_zpse92cd7f4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sarai is a tough girl. All she went through, endured, yet she still puts others before her, she has a soft heart, but she isn’t afraid to kick some ass. I was impressed with her character. Her story broke my heart. Spending her whole teenage/adult life captive, she was willing to do anything to escape her life. She is brave. Victor helps her, but this girl needs no saving. She saves herself. She fights her own battles. I loved watching Victor and Sarai’s relationship develop. It was a slow build, but amazing to read. Sarai brings something out in Victor. Something he’s never felt before. <br><b>“You made me feel real emotions. You unlocked me.”</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/be79b275-1237-4e47-a519-1c07c829447c_zps7f09da9e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425059i/847838.jpg" alt=" photo be79b275-1237-4e47-a519-1c07c829447c_zps7f09da9e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was such an incredible read. It had EVERYTHING. Drama. Action. Suspense. Sex. Emotion. It captivated me. It kept me on my toes, guessing what was going to happen next. I loved all the twists and turns. Just amazing! The ending... I wouldn’t call it a cliffhanger. It wasn’t a conventional HEA, but it sets up nicely for book 2... which I NEED asap!!! One of the best books I’ve read in a while, a must read in my book! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b85500c0-e459-4210-9bdf-ed0b7b5c75a8_zps62d2a4e5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425059i/847839.jpg" alt=" photo b85500c0-e459-4210-9bdf-ed0b7b5c75a8_zps62d2a4e5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4736120060666683256" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_646459436" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646459436" />
    <a title="xrysa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9016476-xrysa"><img alt="xrysa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438615835p2/9016476.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646459436?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2013</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13377172540622788046"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426115i/851084.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Sarai</b><br/><i>Beautiful but defeated and damaged.</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426115i/851085._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Victor</b><br/><i>Can he be her savior?</i><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426115i/851086._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sarai is a 23 year old girl.She's been held as a captive for 9 years.She cant stand witnessing the rapping and the abusing anymore.<b>She has to escape.</b>Yet her only opportunity for a ticket to freedom is an American.He is a cold blooded murderer but given the circumstances she cant be picky so she sneaks into his car threatening him and she is praying that her plan has worked.However back in the compound she left behind her best fr</span>
  <span id="freeText13377172540622788046" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426115i/851084.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Sarai</b><br><i>Beautiful but defeated and damaged.</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426115i/851085._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Victor</b><br><i>Can he be her savior?</i><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426115i/851086._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sarai is a 23 year old girl.She's been held as a captive for 9 years.She cant stand witnessing the rapping and the abusing anymore.<b>She has to escape.</b>Yet her only opportunity for a ticket to freedom is an American.He is a cold blooded murderer but given the circumstances she cant be picky so she sneaks into his car threatening him and she is praying that her plan has worked.However back in the compound she left behind her best friend , Lydia , an angry slut,Izel, and a furious -let's say- boyfriend , Javier.He is brutal and dangerous but he never treated her like the rest of the girls. Sarai always had more civil in comparison to the other captives. Maybe it was because of her beauty or maybe because she wasn’t really abducted.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/587260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>FYI Sarai is not the innocent girl you might give her credit for.She can be dangerous when her life is being threatened but she doesn’t have the intention to hurt anyone.<br><br>Victor has a strange and cold personality but he is her only protection.I liked him a lot not because of his blue-green eyes(yeah maybe that too) but because he is smart and very cautious. I would love to know why he is helping her in first place.In that way he is risking everything and he betrays everyone. Nevertheless he is genius and his plans <b>always</b> work.<br><br>Well now that we all now how Sarai grew up,it has only left to wonder <i>how she will fit into the society again.</i>She is not normal and she will never be.She is a person that can manipulate the others and I have to tell that she is a perfect actress.<br><br>This is a story of <blockquote>
  <b>life</b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>love</b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>trust</b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>and betrayal</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Part of me was so relived with the ending.I thought that everything was over but unfortunately nothing is over yet.<br><br>I loved this book a lot.Their relationship is not your typical love story.It wasn’t even clear if it was love or not.I have to admit that the author's writing style is absolutely amazing.Everything is so detailed and beautiful written.Nothing that you can predict will happen. This is a book that I'd definitely recommend , not only to those who love captive stories but to everyone.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426115ra/851087.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_637860672" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637860672" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637860672?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637860672" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18266575634856838864"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424857i/847250._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> OK. Yeah. I fell for the bad guy.<br/><br/>From the first few pages, <i> Killing Sarai </i> had my undivided attention. Unputdownable! </b><br/><br/>The story here is that of an American girl, Sarai, who was handed off to a Mexican drug dealer at the age of fourteen by her own mother. Her life since then has been one filled with drugs, brutality, murder and slavery. She knows escape is futile - it would be suicide. Out there in the middle of Mexico, there is literally no where she can go. So when an American hit man comes to</span>
  <span id="freeText18266575634856838864" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424857i/847250._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> OK. Yeah. I fell for the bad guy.<br><br>From the first few pages, <i> Killing Sarai </i> had my undivided attention. Unputdownable! </b><br><br>The story here is that of an American girl, Sarai, who was handed off to a Mexican drug dealer at the age of fourteen by her own mother. Her life since then has been one filled with drugs, brutality, murder and slavery. She knows escape is futile - it would be suicide. Out there in the middle of Mexico, there is literally no where she can go. So when an American hit man comes to the compound on business, she sees her way out and takes it.<br><br>All she wants is to get home. But running away has it's consequences. Victor is a cold-blooded, hard man - trained from an early age to be a killer… and now, he's her only hope for survival.<br><br><blockquote> <i> "I need you to help me... I've been a prisoner of Javier's since I was fourteen years old."<br>"And you assume I'm going to help because I am also American," he said simple.<br>I hesitate before I answer, "I-I... well why wouldn't you?"<br>"It is not my business to interfere."<br>"Then what IS your business? I ask with a trace of distaste. "To murder people in cold blood?"<br>"Yes."<br><br>"You know I'm in a lot of danger," I say.<br>"Yes, but that still does not make you my problem."<br>"Are you HUMAN?" I hate him more every time he speaks. "What kind of man would not want to help a defenseless young woman especially when she has escaped her captors and is directly pleading for your help?"<br>He doesn't answer. </i>
</blockquote>  <br><br>I felt myself drawn to Victor's character. He was so intriguing! Always in control, always one step ahead. Smart, calculating, efficient, seemingly ruthless on the outside but I sensed a spark of something… deeper maybe?<br><br>I couldn't tell what his end game was at first but that made sense because I don't think even he knew his end game. He was torn between what he was trained to do, what made sense to do given the world he lived in, but also what his conscience (however far buried it was) was telling him. And something about Sarai was slowly unraveling him.<br><br><blockquote> <i> "In the end, you can only trust yourself. I am not your hero. I am not the other half of your soul who could never let anything bad ever happen to you. Trust your instincts first always, and me, if you choose, last." </i>
</blockquote>  <br><br>Sarai has really had the worst of life handed to her but yet she'd remained quite strong and I was pleasantly surprised to watch her discover her inner badass.<br><br>The world was brutal but the descriptions were never too graphic. It told you just enough to keep you connected and 'in the moment' but never enough to make your stomach turn. Remember, this is a New Adult story so there is some steam, but it's not too detailed. I did wish there had been a little more though but I expect we might see more in the sequel.<br><br>That being said, I loved seeing them slowly give into what they were feeling. It was more of a leap for Victor than Sarai because for him relationships were not only forbidden but simply did not belong in his dangerous lifestyle.<br><br><blockquote> <i> "Despite my growing fear, I still want to be right where I am, trapped in the merciless arms of a killer." </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>The plot was unpredictable and I loved that. It kept me wondering what would happen next and kept surprising me. That being said, it didn't really put my heart in my throat either, but it did keep my attention at all times.<br><br>This is the kind of story that makes you just have to keep flipping the pages. The pacing is fast, the writing is fluid, the story is engaging and the characters are intriguing. All in all, it's a fabulous read if you're looking for something totally 'different'. I really enjoyed it!<br><br>The ending… ho boy! It leaves you desperately wanting more but at the same time, I got the feeling that it would all be okay in the end. Basically, there is a slight cliffhanger. It wasn't a 'holy shit' kind of ending, but rather just one that clearly left a lot more to the story. And there is a note at the end that says that Victor and Sarai's story will continue in the sequel which is to be released later in 2013. I can't wait!<br><br>4.5 stars<br><br><b> CASTING: I think I found my Victor....<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424857i/847251._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424857i/847252._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Exclusive Excerpt here:<br>✦ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/killing-sarai-ja-redmerski/">http://aestasbookblog.com/killing-sar...</a> </b><br><br><i> Sarai was only fourteen when her mother uprooted her to live in Mexico with a notorious drug lord. Over time she forgot what it was like to live a normal life, but she never let go of her hope to escape the compound where she has been held for the past nine years.<br><br>Victor is a cold-blooded assassin who, like Sarai, has known only death and violence since he was a young boy. When Victor arrives at the compound to collect details and payment for a hit, Sarai sees him as her only opportunity for escape. But things don’t go as planned and instead of finding transport back to Tucson, she finds herself free from one dangerous man and caught in the clutches of another.<br><br>While on the run, Victor strays from his primal nature as he succumbs to his conscience and resolves to help Sarai. As they grow closer, he finds himself willing to risk everything to keep her alive; even his relationship with his devoted brother and liaison, Niklas, who now like everyone else wants Sarai dead.<br><br>As Victor and Sarai slowly build a trust, the differences between them seem to lessen, and an unlikely attraction intensifies. But Victor’s brutal skills and experience may not be enough in the end to save her, as the power she unknowingly holds over him may ultimately be what gets her killed.<br><br>This is their story… </i><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="18266575634856838864" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_648176191" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/648176191" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/648176191?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=on-going-series">on-going-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=rom-suspense">rom-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer648176191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2347953956275692733"><i>
  <b>1.5 STARS</b>
</i><br/><br/>Anyone up for some Jeopardy?<br/><br/>I'll take familiar blurbs for 200, Alex.<br/><br/><a href='http://www.flickr.com/photos/99937251@N03/9455596059/' title='clue-1 by ashwednesdaylee, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426361i/851951.jpg' width='300' height='225' alt='clue-1' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Um...<br/><br/>Okay let's pause for an awkward second and admire the pink, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16029994-sins-needles?ac=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>tattooed elephant named Caithness Macbeth </a>in the room.<br/><br/>...<br/><br/>Everyone good?<br/><br/>Don't get me wrong, this is a totally different story (more along the lines of <i>Leon: The Professional</i> but not as good), but given the distant yet still noticeable similarities with a favorite series and my gripes against this book, I'm having a hard time thinking of what I liked</span>
  <span id="freeText2347953956275692733" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>1.5 STARS</b>
</i><br><br>Anyone up for some Jeopardy?<br><br>I'll take familiar blurbs for 200, Alex.<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/99937251@N03/9455596059/" title="clue-1 by ashwednesdaylee, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426361i/851951.jpg" width="300" height="225" alt="clue-1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Um...<br><br>Okay let's pause for an awkward second and admire the pink, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16029994-sins-needles?ac=1" rel="nofollow noopener">tattooed elephant named Caithness Macbeth </a>in the room.<br><br>...<br><br>Everyone good?<br><br>Don't get me wrong, this is a totally different story (more along the lines of <i>Leon: The Professional</i> but not as good), but given the distant yet still noticeable similarities with a favorite series and my gripes against this book, I'm having a hard time thinking of what I liked about it. Because for some reason, it felt like I watched a B-movie about assassins, ham-acted out by B-actors filmed on the gaudiest locations.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>He leaves it at that and walks into the room where I continue to follow and once I'm inside, the beauty of it takes my breath away. <u>There are four life-sized statues of Greek women wearing flowing gowns, standing tall in all four corners of this round, dome-shaped room.To my right another wall-sized window overlooks the turbulent ocean and in front of it, sitting proudly on display is the most beautiful piano I've ever seen.</u>
</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>That's where Victor, our hero, lives. And no he is not a centuries old vampire. <br><br>I think my major issue was everything about this story was executed half-baked and half-heartedly. There's a great dearth of grit and tension in the storytelling, Something about the themes this book chose to deal with need to be delivered with a certain panache; a brave balls-out, swagger where it came out short of in every way. <br><br>I always felt like it was holding back, trying not to get too offensive. Take for example the scene in LA where they were alone with Arthur Hamburg <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ where the man propositions them to have sex in front of him while he watches followed by the guy sucking off Victor. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Which didn't happen because, as in any PG-13 movie, the hero finds a way to save the day. I'm not a pervert (most of the times) just out for the smut factor, but if you're going to set your story with off-beat characters with intense backstories, you can't expect me to not complain when it doesn't deliver on the promised potential when the time comes. <br><br>Or maybe it's just because I've seen these issues handled better and given the proper edge in the treatment, elsewhere?<br><br>I have the most difficult time dealing with Sarai. Her character profile is so confusing. She pities Izel one moment, only to be glad<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ to watch her die <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, several chapters after. She doesn't act like someone who has been "enslaved" for 9 years, easily adapting to the circumstances Victor throws at her. And I don't understand why the author made her "special" in Javier's harem, because this effectively takes out any hope of sympathy I may have for her. Her initial guilt over enjoying all sorts of luxury (Except wearing a bra. Dear gad, the travesty!) being Javier's favorite while the rest of the harem suffers went forgotten. With not one iota of guilt after assuming the Izabel persona. And this circular argument that just made my nose bleed:<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I hated Javier. I hated that even though he never raped me, at least not like you expect rape to happen; he knew at first I was unwilling, that I only gave in to him because I was afraid and yet he still had sex with me and I say that's rape. But I hated him and I hated that I gave myself to a man that I did not want.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><b>WHAT IN THE EVER LIVING FUCK?!</b><br><br>There's something strange in the way the dialogue of the characters are phrased. This is told in alternating POVs between Sarai and Victor with very little to distinguish one POV from the other. But my major issue is that there are lengths of dialogue (that are actually lengthy monologues, thinking back) that didn't sound conversational at all. It's as if the characters are reading their lines off a script. A badly written script at that. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"What kind of man would not want to help a defenseless young woman out of a life of bondage and violence, especially when she has escaped her captors and is directly pleading for your help?"</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Who talks like that? Seriously?<br><br>And everything else I said in my status updates because I'm already tired of hearing my own voice in my head and I don't want to talk about the piano playing and the chest beating while crying and the lukewarm sex anymore.<br><br>I'm sorry but it seems I am the kind of reader who doesn't get impressed by throwing in gunfights and dead bodies and shocking gestures into the story for the sake of. What, someone shoves his hand in a girl's cunny and you expect me to gasp in surprise and call this edgy and gritty? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426361ra/851952.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2347953956275692733" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_646254614" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646254614" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646254614?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=dark-read">dark-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=keeper-shelf">keeper-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=books-with-an-edge">books-with-an-edge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646254614" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17964000221580537427"><b>
  <i>5 Completely Enthralling Stars</i>
</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>I don't think that this thing between us is love, or even lust. It's something else, something powerful and unmistakable that neither of us have been able to ignore. But it doesn't have a face. Or a name.</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426086i/850956.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>I am discipline. Sarai is rage.</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This book was a roller coaster of emotions that I wished would never end.<br/>I still can't exactly put into words everything that I felt about this book.<br/><br/>I went from<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850957.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>to<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850958.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>to<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808101.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>to<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850959.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>and back to<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850957.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The writing was brilliant. The story was "unab</span>
  <span id="freeText17964000221580537427" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>5 Completely Enthralling Stars</i>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>I don't think that this thing between us is love, or even lust. It's something else, something powerful and unmistakable that neither of us have been able to ignore. But it doesn't have a face. Or a name.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426086i/850956.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>I am discipline. Sarai is rage.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book was a roller coaster of emotions that I wished would never end.<br>I still can't exactly put into words everything that I felt about this book.<br><br>I went from<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850957.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>to<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850958.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>to<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>to<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850959.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and back to<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850957.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The writing was brilliant. The story was "unable to put the book down for even a second" good. It was unlike anything I've read in a long, long time. <br><br><b>Victor</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850960.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Victor was an enigma. The author did such an amazing job with characterization that the reader got both not enough of Victor that he had this air of mystery about him the entire book, and yet give us just enough crumbs that made him incredibly endearing despite his coldness at the same time. He was scary, he was mysterious, he was also so DAMN HAWT! <br><br><b>Syrai</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426086ra/850961.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Syrai was such an incredible heroine. She was both vulnerable yet completely kick-ass. She went through hell for nine years. She has seen things that no child should ever have to see, and been through horrors. Never having a childhood, she went from one hell into a whole different one. When she escapes the captivity through a mysterious stranger she knows only as Victor. For a 23 year old, and having been through as much as she had, she still managed to come off as so incredibly strong.<br><br>The story is not your fairy tale romance. It is not sunshine and rainbows and unicorns. It's dark, twisted, gritty, and sucks you in from the very first page.<br><br>The romance builds realistically over time. I was so happy to see that the author did that, because had it been quicker or lust at first sight it would not have done these amazing characters justice. The majority of this book is the suspense and action, and it doesn't disappoint in either case. It's fast paced, and keeps you on the edge of your seat until the very last page.<br><br>The ending I felt was very fitting. It was not exactly a cliffhanger, though it is quite clear that their story is far from finished. As much as I would have loved a HEA, it would not have been true to the story to give Sarai and Victor one at that point of the book.<br><br>__________________________________________________________<br>My thoughts when I just finished the book:<br><i><br>Holy shit! This book!<br>I have no words...<br>No really! I need to get my shit together and gather my wits before I write a review...<br>I need a fucking moment here!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426086i/850962.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17964000221580537427" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_639765425" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639765425" />
    <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites"><img alt="Alexis *Reality Bites*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1404308282p2/5587514.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

<div id="review_1146405392" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1146405392" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1146405392?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Melanie by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/22889537-lainey">Lainey</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=erotic-scenes">erotic-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146405392" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13356753857021733995"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There is a stark difference between fear and uncertainty, Sarai. You fear nothing but are uncertain of everything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I have had this book recommended to me a lot over the years. But the thing is, dipping into older published dark romance normally isn’t the best experience, so I’ve put off this 2013 publication for a while. But honestly? This actually was a really enthralling read that held up really well in 2018. And I am really excited to continue on with the series. <br/><br/>➽ <b>Sarai</b> - Curren</span>
  <span id="freeText13356753857021733995" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There is a stark difference between fear and uncertainty, Sarai. You fear nothing but are uncertain of everything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />I have had this book recommended to me a lot over the years. But the thing is, dipping into older published dark romance normally isn’t the best experience, so I’ve put off this 2013 publication for a while. But honestly? This actually was a really enthralling read that held up really well in 2018. And I am really excited to continue on with the series. <br /><br />➽ <b>Sarai</b> - Currently is twenty-three but was fourteen when her mom gave her to a drug lord. Sarai starts the book in captivity, as a sex slave of the leader of this organization that is in Mexico. And one day at the compound, she hears the first American accent she has heard in years and takes the opportunity to try for her freedom once and for all. <br /><br />➽ <b>Victor</b> - An assassin who has only known bloodshed his entire life. But when he finds a girl in the backseat of his vehicle, he feels a soft spot for her, while also understanding that he could use her as leverage against a very powerful drug lord. <br /><br />And from there these two’s paths are intertwined and their lives are changed forever. Neither one has ever really known what love is, and never really let anyone in before. But together, they form a really unexpected friendship and partnership. Also, neither one of them can give up on revenge and decide that maybe together they can right the wrongs that have been done against them. <br /><br />So, I read this book for the <a href="https://twitter.com/search?q=%23smutathon&amp;src=typd" rel="nofollow noopener">#smutathon</a> challenge of “slow burn” and holy shit was this the perfect fit for the category. You all, I was begging, wishing, praying, for these two to just realize that they like each other. Like, this is the most slow burn book of all slow burns! But the angst and wanting is really expertly done and make you totally unable to put this book down. <br /><br />This is a darker book, so please use caution while reading. <b>Content and trigger warnings</b> for sex trafficking, slavery, kidnapping, murder, death, loss of a loved one, blood depictions, talk of sexual assault, talk of rape, talk of pedophilia, animal death, parental abuse, abandonment, torture, and fatphobic comments. Also, I mean, the romance in this could maybe be a little Stockholm syndrome, even though I didn’t feel that way, I can totally see how it could be perceived as such. And obviously there is a huge power imbalance between Victor and Sarai. <br /><br />But I do need to talk about the reason I did give this three stars, and that’s because one of the villains in this book, who I’m guessing is going to be a really big villain in the next books, is not only queer, but he is constantly villainized for being fat. And this is exactly why going back and reading older dark romances are normally painful, because they constantly use hurtful tropes like this. And this in no way gets a free pass because it’s older, this is a disgusting trope that I will never be here for, regardless of the year of publication. Miss me with this nasty villainization of queer and fat people, when you could easily just villainize the man for being a rapist. <br /><br />Overall, this is a really hard book to put down, and there is action on every page. I really enjoyed reading this one (besides the hot mess in the paragraph above this one). I totally plan to continue on, even if I’m a little apprehensive about the villain, but Sarai and Victor just have me feeling weak and I need to know what happens to them at the end of this story. <br /><br /><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a><br /><br />I read this for <a href="https://twitter.com/search?q=%23smutathon&amp;src=typd" rel="nofollow noopener">#smutathon</a>, which is being hosted by <a href="https://t.co/jYqsnNfDN8" rel="nofollow noopener">Lainey</a> and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/Rileymarie1196" rel="nofollow noopener">Riley</a>! ❤</span>
  <a data-text-id="13356753857021733995" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1070190757" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4737803024296938807"><b>5 **<u>kick-ass</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443113641i/16319883.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Despite my growing fear, I still want to be right where I am, trapped in the merciless arms of a killer.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>My kind of book. I can't even begin to tell you how right this read was for me. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20559676-killing-sarai' rel='nofollow noopener'>Killing Sarai</a> is one of those stories that just clicked with me from the first page. Angst, action, edge of the seat suspense and a subtly developed romance story. None of that insta-lust nonsense. <br/><br/>First and foremost I have to thank my dear friend Jasmine for recommending me this s</span>
  <span id="freeText4737803024296938807" style="display:none"><b>5 **<u>kick-ass</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443113641i/16319883.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Despite my growing fear, I still want to be right where I am, trapped in the merciless arms of a killer.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>My kind of book. I can't even begin to tell you how right this read was for me. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20559676-killing-sarai" rel="nofollow noopener">Killing Sarai</a> is one of those stories that just clicked with me from the first page. Angst, action, edge of the seat suspense and a subtly developed romance story. None of that insta-lust nonsense. <br><br>First and foremost I have to thank my dear friend Jasmine for recommending me this series. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5437976.J_A_Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">J.A. Redmerski</a> is a completely new author for me and I'm pretty confident to say I'm a fan after only reading one book.<br><br>Let's talk story...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443282538i/16343531.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Sarai</b> has been living a life of captivity since she was fourteen years old. Nine years ago her mother took her to Mexico and ever since she was a drug lord's "favourite". With no way to escape she resigned herself to the life she was given, accepted her fate and played along. That is until one day an American arrives at the compound. The dormant fight rises in her and she uses her chance to flee.<br><br><b>Victor Faust</b> is an assassin. Cool, collected and very much in control of his world. Until the chatty girl hides in the back of his car after a meeting with a client. He starts to make decisions that threaten his life, his work and the armor around his person.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I don’t think this thing between us is love, or even lust. It’s something else, something powerful and unmistakable that neither of us have been able to ignore. But it doesn’t have a face.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This is not a book about redemption or saving each other from a bad faith. In fact once Victor and Sarai meet their journey leads them even deeper down the rabbit hole. Both have lead lives commonly described as ‘not normal’. Victor joined ‘the Order’ when he was nine years old and was subsequently trained to become who he is now. Sarai grew up in a trailer park with a drug addict mother. After that, nine years of seeing violence, rape and crime desensitised her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443121055i/16320519.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For all intents and purposes both main characters are damaged in their own way. Together they create a loveable mix of dysfunction and ruthlessness. I was so fascinated by the way the author managed to fit them together like a puzzle. Step by step Sarai puts cracks in Victor’s hardened exterior and Victor is just unable to pull the trigger on the girl and the connection they developed.<br><br>They are by far the most captivating couple I have met in a long time. Even though the book is written in both their POVs we learn very little about Victor and he stays an enigma for the most part. Stoic and very silent. Well, and Sarai constantly managed to surprise me with her strength and astounding ability to cope.<br><br>Of course they have to deal with a lot of trouble. Drug lords, employers, their own stubbornness, reckless behaviour and family members. Don't get me started on the somewhat open ending...luckily the next four books are already published. ;D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Killing Sarai</i> is the first book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/106345-in-the-company-of-killers" rel="nofollow noopener">In the Company of Killers Series</a> and is not a standalone read. Victor and Sarai's story continues with <i>Reviving Izabel</i>. I can only recommend picking up this book for the excellent writing and the spellbinding, action packed story alone. But if you also love a kick-ass heroine and a merciless assassin then I really don’t know what you are waiting for. READ THE BOOK!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441631277i/16131398.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_639182005" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639182005" />
    <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie"><img alt="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505392311p2/11641363.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/639182005?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=give-this-author-a-bells">give-this-author-a-bells</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=gritty-writing">gritty-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=human-trafficking">human-trafficking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=crime-mystery">crime-mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer639182005" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12509966248397728786"><b>5 Fast Paced and Gripping Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425051i/847803._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sarai has been held captive for nines years, subjected to the whims of a mad man. She has never given up hope of escape, so when she sees an american visitor, something that's never happened before, she takes a chance and risks her life for freedom.<br/><br/>But nothing is always as it seems. Gun in hand, Sarai forces Victor the american visitor to take her to the american border. But Victor isn't the salvation Sarai was looking for, she realises that she may have left he</span>
  <span id="freeText12509966248397728786" style="display:none"><b>5 Fast Paced and Gripping Stars!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425051i/847803._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sarai has been held captive for nines years, subjected to the whims of a mad man. She has never given up hope of escape, so when she sees an american visitor, something that's never happened before, she takes a chance and risks her life for freedom.<br><br>But nothing is always as it seems. Gun in hand, Sarai forces Victor the american visitor to take her to the american border. But Victor isn't the salvation Sarai was looking for, she realises that she may have left her captivity, but she has thrown herself in to a much more dire situation. the man she is with is a killer, and wouldn't think twice before ending her life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425051i/847804.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In one single moment it seems as if her life is about to end. But Victor surprises her, surprises even himself by doing exactly what he has been trained not to do. Sarai is an enigma to him, he feels drawn to her. He realises that she is a threat to him, but cannot decide how to remedy this problem even though it is quite obvious.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425051i/847805.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Victor and Sarai journey is one filled with pain and uncertainty but also self discovery. Sarai begins to find the strength inside herself the longer she is with Victor. She may not be the ideal woman or the woman society expects her to be. But she becomes a woman of her circumstances, she becomes warrior no longer a victim. She learns to love, although she may not know it, this becomes her strength. Yes, at times she is scared but she no longer cowers in fright, but stands up and faces the challenge.<br><br>Victor feels protective of Sarai, something he has never felt for any woman before. Her pain is something he takes no joy in, he wants her to be safe, have a chance at happiness, a good life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425051i/847806.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Victor's life scares Sarai, but not enough for her to not want to be around him. She sees a different side to him, he doesn't show it often, but it's there. Every glimpse she gets, proves to her that Victor has a heart although he might not want her to see it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425051i/847807.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a fast paced, gripping and thrilling novel. It will keep you on the edge of your seat, there are surprises at every turn of your digital page. I truly have never read a book like this before, Miss Redmerski you have been holding out on us! It will leave you craving more, leave you wanting to find another book that will match the absolute genuis that J.A Redmerski has created!<br><br>I love books that are narrated in the first person, I think it feeds the need I have to become the character. It makes it so much easier to pretend that it's actually me that's playing the character! Haha! The fact that I got to read it form the hero's POV as well made the book an absolutely satisfying read!<br><br>This is one of those books where you'll find yourself wanting a physical copy, signed proof that you didn't dream this wonderful story.</span>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_645698115" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/645698115" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/645698115?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=i-like-it-dark-and-twisted">i-like-it-dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer645698115" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11892165555452811336"><b>
  <i>”I am discipline. Sarai is rage. I am aware of my choices at all times. Sarai’s choices are more aware of her, lying in wait to decide for her based on the severity of her mood with no intention in leaving her any conscious control over it.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>J.A. Redmerski’s <i>Sarai</i> is nothing like her hit novel <i>The Edge of Never</i> which I loved. This story is an entirely different animal. I read the book the first day it was released but sat on my review because I wasn’t sure I could come up with enough adjectiv</span>
  <span id="freeText11892165555452811336" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”I am discipline. Sarai is rage. I am aware of my choices at all times. Sarai’s choices are more aware of her, lying in wait to decide for her based on the severity of her mood with no intention in leaving her any conscious control over it.”</i>
</b><br><br>J.A. Redmerski’s <i>Sarai</i> is nothing like her hit novel <i>The Edge of Never</i> which I loved. This story is an entirely different animal. I read the book the first day it was released but sat on my review because I wasn’t sure I could come up with enough adjectives to express to a reader how <b>FANTASTIC</b> this story actually is. <br><br>This book is nonstop action there is no down time in the story to take a break. Please block out a fair amount of time to read this book because you will NOT want to stop at all! The writing, the characters, the alternating povs and the story were completely consuming. <br><br>The main character Sarai rocks! She is one hell of a female lead. She is strong, damaged, smart and any reader will fall completely in love with her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426004i/850718._SX540_.jpg" width="440" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>”She shows all the signs of having lost the ability to react to fear and danger appropriately. She is numb to danger and that in itself is a death sentence.”</i>
</b><br><br>Sarai’s inner dialogue was perfection and made me feel like I was in fact on the run with Sarai from the horrible Javier in the car with the dangerous Victor. <br><br><b>
  <i>”Like it or not, Victor is my only protection until I can get over that border and I’m going to stick with him as long as I can regardless of my desperate need to get away from him, too.”~Sarai</i>
</b><br><br>So it seems that Sarai’s way out of her nine years of captivity from a drug lord in Mexico is an American who seems to be a cold blooded contract murderer. Victor NEVER does friendships or relationships.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426004i/850719.jpg" width="340" height="440" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The way Victor’s character unfolded was so well done. The way Victor teetered on the edge of staying true to his brother and his Order while protecting Sarai was so exciting.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426004i/850720._SY540_.jpg" width="340" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>”And I don’t kill innocent people.” <br><br>Silence fills the small space between us.<br><br>“No one is innocent,” I snap, surprising myself. “Least of all me.”</i>
</b><br><br>Sexual tension starts to rise while the couple faces one intense situation after another all the while Victor has to stay on track with his employer, his brother and his Order. A reader finds themselves falling hard for this couple to find a way to stay together even if it’s not for the best.<br><br>Once you hit the end of the story, you won’t be left hanging on a cliff but actually excited for the continuation and hopes of what the next book will hold for these two characters.<br><br><b>
  <i>”This goes against everything I am, Sarai,” he says and then kisses me.<br>“No, it doesn’t,” I whisper and kiss him back. “It’s you becoming more of who you really are.”</i>
</b><br><br>Overall the ending is not your typical hea. Although a reader is left excited for the next book. <br><br>J.A. Redmerski this book left me...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395714ra/762194.gif" width="340" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Go forth and get lost in this story!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="11892165555452811336" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13221481389171651662" style="display:none"><b>I LOVE THIS NEW COVER!!!! OH.MY.GOD!!! It's time to order my paperback :D</b><br><br><b>6 Stars, no 15 Million STARS!!!!</b><br><br>Full review with guest post J.A. Redmerski - &gt; <a href="http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline’s Reads</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/wgPtucJ" rel="nofollow noopener">
