</a><br><br><b>The very first thing I need to say is that I absolutely, with my heart and every fiber in my body LOVED LOVED … did I say LOVE? YES! LOVED <i>Killing Sarai</i></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/kJCtxPy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425048i/847788.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yup, <i>Killing Sarai</i> is up there with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483778459" rel="nofollow noopener">Hopeless</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/467165603" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Disaster</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/585854939" rel="nofollow noopener">Real</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610988938" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled</a>. I don’t have that many spots on my top favorites, but <i>Killing Sarai</i> deserves that spot. Honestly, I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/495221174" rel="nofollow noopener">The Edge of Never</a> and yes I had expectations from J.A. Redmerski, but my expectations were met by tenfold!<br><br><b>[Cliff-notes version of my review]</b><br><br>I’m going to do a lot gushing, so, if you want something short and sweet, here it is…<br><br>Here is my version of Victor<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/1O2XCwe" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425048i/847789.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Here is my version of Sarai<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/ClVIt1j" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425048i/847790.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And there is my short version of review. I went into <i>Killing Sarai</i> without knowing anything and if you are like me, just do it BUT if you need a review, then proceed.<br><br><b>[Summary]</b><br><br>Sarai was taken to Mexico when she was 14 years old. Her mom left her with a drug lord, Javier. Sarai is Javier’s favorite. Sarai is now 23 and over hears an American, Victor, the first time in 9 years she lands a perfect opporunity. She takes quick action and sneaks out of her compound also known as her prison and hides in the American’s car. Victor is a hitman, he’s highly professional and doesn’t let his emotions comprise his situation ever. Javier hired Victor to take out a hit, but on his way to his target, he soon finds his stowaway and doesn’t know what to do with her. <br><br><b>[Review]</b><br><br><b>
  <i>…while peering into my eyes, though beyond them. I wonder what he’s looking for in their depths. Whatever it is, I hope he never finds it so that we can stay like this forever.</i>
</b><br><br>I absolutely loved Sarai and Victor. She was the perfect Heroine and Victor was the perfect Hero, also known as the future father of my child and a book boyfriend. You.feel.for.Sarai. Her innocence was taken from her and all she has ever known was to do what she had to do to survive yet she’s human and has inner conflicts. I understood Sarai completely. I felt like I was her, I felt like I was asking the same questions and I just wanted to help her! <br><br><b>
  <i>There is a stark difference between fear and uncertainty, Sarai. You fear nothing but are uncertain of everything.</i>
</b><br><br>Then, there’s cold, calculating Victor who is just 100% lickable and edible. I don’t know how to describe him. There’s just something so sexy about a calm, confident, yet deadly man.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/GMhMZb4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425048ra/847791.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>I am attracted to him. I do have a strange, unfamiliar feelings for him. And I hate it!</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/SjN39vq" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425048i/847792.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me just say, this read isn’t steamy, but oh you could cut the sexual tension with a knife and I love it! In the beginning Sarai is just trying to find her way back to America and Victor is well to me a huge blank. We don’t really understand what goes on until later and it’s just a perfect dance of giving me what I need instead of what I want. I like this and I love the tension.<br><br><b>
  <i>I feel like a toy and Victor knows every button on me which to push, to touch, in order to make me do whatever he wants, feel whatever he wants me to feel. And I don’t mind.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/KsuPtGL" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425048i/847793.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>My emotions throughout the read…<br><br>At 1% I’m like oh damn… from page 1 I was hooked<br><br>At 12% I felt like I was going to read something epic<br><br>At 32% my mind is blown away<br><br>At 74% I am just glued to my tablet and I don’t want the read to end<br><br>At 82% I have no f@cking clue to what’s going on, but I love it<br><br>At 100%.... I just had a book orgasm</b><br><br>What made me love Killing Sarai so much was the natural progression of Sarai and Victor’s from beginning to end . I can’t tell you enough how I love character build-up and relationships forming from trust, understanding and sometimes self-sacrifice, instead of just pure lust. You will not know what happens from start to finish and it was perfect.<br><br><br>I don’t really want to recap the plot too much. I feel you should go into this read with little in mind. Just know while reading it, there will be a lot of tension, dramatic situations, shooting, chasing, dying and just mind f&amp;cks throughout the way.<br><br>Oh and there is a cliff-hanger, kind of. I mean the ending opens to book 2, Reviving Izabel, but I was okay with it. It's an open cliff-hanger, but you are left very satisfied. I know, I hate cliffys too, but this one isn't bad. I promise!<br><br><b>
  <i>I am grateful… for everything you’ve done for me. I guess in the end none of it will really matter, not saving my life or sparing it. But I’ll always be grateful to you.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/LjnruvA" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425048i/847794.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh and when Victor said …<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[But you did something else that no one else ever could…You made me feel real emotions. You unlocked me.<br><br>And I watch her unlike I’ve ever watched her before. She owns me in this moment <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I think I just fainted and died right there!<br><br>RATING<br><br><b>6++++++ Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/7x7wpxX" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_651561297" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/651561297" />
    <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9138738-georgia"><img alt="Georgia ♥ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377186210p2/9138738.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/651561297?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Georgia ♥  by: </span>
      Soraya Naomi &amp; Kristina
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=abused-hero-or-and-heroine">abused-hero-or-and-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=sobbing-mess">sobbing-mess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=suspense-mystery">suspense-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=another-freaking-cliffhanger">another-freaking-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=favourite-cause-it-is-unique">favourite-cause-it-is-unique</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking">the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer651561297" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8505529357929767536"><b>LIFE<br/><br/>DEATH<br/><br/>PASSION</b><br/><br/><b>5 and beyond MIND-BLOWING Stars<br/><br/><i>...such is the life I lead, a dark and lonely path lined only with the solitude of death.</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426857i/853239.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What is a person to do when forced to its limits? What becomes of victims of abuse when they live through it daily for years? Are we a product of our environment, shaped and molded of the circumstances around us, adapted and programmed to survive no matter the cost? And what is the line that differentiates bad and good?<br/><br/>Frankly, there is no black and white. Just </span>
  <span id="freeText8505529357929767536" style="display:none"><b>LIFE<br><br>DEATH<br><br>PASSION</b><br><br><b>5 and beyond MIND-BLOWING Stars<br><br><i>...such is the life I lead, a dark and lonely path lined only with the solitude of death.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426857i/853239.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What is a person to do when forced to its limits? What becomes of victims of abuse when they live through it daily for years? Are we a product of our environment, shaped and molded of the circumstances around us, adapted and programmed to survive no matter the cost? And what is the line that differentiates bad and good?<br><br>Frankly, there is no black and white. Just a million shades of grey in-between...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426857i/853240.png" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a whole world out there hidden beneath expensive clothes and glamorous parties. A world of depravity, abuse, slavery. And death. It's always death. Someone who deals in it, takes pleasure, inflicts, fights against it. It's up to the person to decide on which side of the gun will stand and who will walk away alive.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/647354.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Sarai</b> has been a slave for the last 9 years. Her own mother sold her when she was fourteen, for her next fix, to a Mexican drug lord. She has a plan to escape and the American Assassin that her captor hired will be her way out. She doesn't suspect that while she can escape slavery she can't escape this new person that she is. A woman molded through fire, a wounded animal, angry and despaired, pained and damaged.<br><br><i>
  <b>“I fear everything. What tomorrow will bring and if I’ll be alive to see the end of it. I’m afraid of Javier or anyone else coming through that door and killing me in my sleep. I’m afraid of never being able to live a normal life. I don’t even know what normal feels like anymore.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424862i/847265._SX540_.png" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Victor</b> is a trained killer since he was 9 years old and he accomplished his first hit when he was 13. A member of the Order, a secret organization of assassins he always has an agenda. Ruthless, methodical, cold, a weapon loaded to kill he will find his lost consciousness in the eyes of a girl hidden in the backseat of his car. <br><br>But he isn't born a savior. He is not a white knight. His instincts are too raw for that and the kind of life that he has led, has him living on edge, kill or be killed, always ready for the next hit.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426857i/853241.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thrown together by circumstance and drawn to each other like moths to flame, these two damaged people with no hope for a future, are going to forge their own path, staying alive, healing the wounds that still bleed and just accept all the scars they collected along the way. But in the end they will have to sacrifice all their emotions to logic and stay alive to fight another day and for a future. <br><br><i>
  <b>“But you did something else that no one else ever could.” His features soften and my heart is slowly melting. “You made me feel real emotions. You unlocked me.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426857ra/853242.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A punch to the gut, a dark story, powerful, gritty, raw and emotional, a journey to the dark side of the human soul, where there are not good and bad choices and you just try and make the most of a horrible situation. A world of kids trained to kill, girls sold to powerful madmen, facades, lies and money. A mind-blowing, unique book that will make you uncomfortable and will open your eyes. You will fall in love with a hired gun, sympathize with the devil and bawl your eyes out for a young girl who prefers to be a killer than return to a normal life that holds no meaning to her anymore.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5437976.J_A__Redmerski" title="J.A. Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">J.A. Redmerski</a> weaves an exceptional story that you won't be able to put down, so much different than her previous work, simple in its inception but unbelievably complex as only a human soul and mind can be. Looking forward to the continuation of Sarai and Victor's story, not to the light but to an acceptable state of darkness where they are comfortable to hide their fears and put their demons to rest without looking over their shoulders. <br><br>Because some people are meant to live as shadows...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426857i/853243._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And decide who gets to live with their last bullet...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426857ra/853244.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="8505529357929767536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1068826837?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jasmine by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1068826837" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2700667500403128594"><b>5 MR AMERICAN STARS! ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421725.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I am not your hero. I am not the other half of your soul who could never let anything bad ever happen to you. Trust your instincts first always, and me, if you choose, last."</i>
</b><br/><br/>This book had all the elements that I <b>LOVED</b> in a romance suspense/thriller book that it was an <b>absolute no-brainer</b> that this would be a winner for me. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> Assassins <- BAMF in suits with guns and multilingual (A lot of bonus points here!!)<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <s>Michael Fassbender</s> Victor <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> BAMF heroine<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> Dual POV (HECK YEA</span>
  <span id="freeText2700667500403128594" style="display:none"><b>5 MR AMERICAN STARS! ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421725.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I am not your hero. I am not the other half of your soul who could never let anything bad ever happen to you. Trust your instincts first always, and me, if you choose, last."</i>
</b><br><br>This book had all the elements that I <b>LOVED</b> in a romance suspense/thriller book that it was an <b>absolute no-brainer</b> that this would be a winner for me. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Assassins &lt;- BAMF in suits with guns and multilingual (A lot of bonus points here!!)<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <s>Michael Fassbender</s> Victor <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> BAMF heroine<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Dual POV (HECK YEA!) <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Nail-biting suspense &amp; heart-pounding action that induced severe heart palpitations <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412778279i/11421726.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Hot steamy scenes<br><br>Put all of them together and.. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/540974.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>WINNER WINNER CHICKEN DINNER, JASMINE IS A HAPPY READER!! <s>Wow that actually rhymed</s><br><br>*********<br><br><b>Killing Sarai</b> is about our heroine, <b>Sarai</b> who has been a captive under a Mexican drug lord for 9 years. She finally made her escape one night when Mr American, <b>Victor</b> showed up at the Mexican compound and Sarai saw that as her golden ticket out. But is Mr American actually a kind, loving man who's gonna save this poor innocent girl from the clutches of the drug lord? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412781222ra/11422162.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Trained to be a cold, detached assassin since the age of thirteen, Victor is the Number One in the Order and has never failed a mission. But with Sarai, he's breaking all the rules he's ever known and finds himself with a conscience to protect her. <br><br><i>When the odds start to stack against them and loyalties are questioned, both Sarai and Victor battle to learn on who can be trusted ultimately.</i><br><br>********* <br><br>HOLY FAN-FUCKING-TASTIC THIS READ. This book was as awesome as watching a movie in my head! Of course, <b>Fassbander is the PERFECT cast in my mind as Victor</b> (eventhough he was initially referred as Mr American, Victor is of German heritage which makes Fassbender the perfect choice) and boy did my mind enjoy it A LOT! It pretty much amplified my experience and love for this read, so THANK YOU Michael Fassbender for graciously walking on our planet! ♥♥<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412781222ra/11422163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As y'all know, I love me a BAMF heroine who's ready to take shit and give it back twice as much. Sarai was a fighter, that's for sure. <b>I loved her resilience but I also loved that she was broken.</b> A strong heroine doesn't mean that she has less fears, but to me, a strong one is one that is willing to acknowledge her fears and face them. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"The things I've admitted are things that have haunted me for the longest time. They've been buried in my soul, burning through to the very core of me, rendering me emotionless and turning me into someone entirely different than I was supposed to be."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/590022.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also when the <b>romance falls in the backburner for me</b> in a suspense/thriller read, I <i>definitely</i> know that the book will work for me. Yes I'm a romance junkie, but I'm a dark/suspense/thriller junkie first ;) And with this one, the <b>suspense gripped me</b> and brought me on a <b>fast-paced thrilling ride</b> because it was <b>completely un-putdownable.</b> <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"The first kill is always the hardest, the one you never forget. But the first kill is also what drops the chances of living a normal life by half."</i>
</blockquote><br>*********<br><br>I was in the minority who didn't fully enjoyed Redmerski's other work, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081272.The_Edge_of_Never__The_Edge_of_Never___1_" title="The Edge of Never (The Edge of Never, #1) by J.A. Redmerski" rel="nofollow noopener">The Edge of Never</a>, but with <b>Killing Sarai</b>, THIS is a whole different ballgame and it was a BEAST! <br><br>JA Redmerski still brought out her <b>exceptional writing</b> with this one and added on with a <b>tinge of romance plus loads of suspense &amp; thrill with badass characters</b>, this book is making its way to the top of my dark thriller reads shelf! <br><br>I can't wait to get my grabby hands on the rest of the series and I suggest you all do the same if you <s>have been living under the rock like me</s> haven't pick this series up yet! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394155858ra/8815360.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A shoutout of thanks to the ever-awesome <b>Feifei</b> for recc'ing this one to me because otherwise I'd be missing out on an amazeball series! ♥ And also <b>thanks to all my other ladies</b> who got me excited for this read when I started picking it up, you ladies are AH-MAZING! Mwahs! ♥♥<br></span>

<div id="review_638430540" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/638430540" />
    <a title="Renee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12732363-renee"><img alt="Renee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596939182p2/12732363.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/638430540?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Renee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Renee" href="/user/show/12732363-renee">Renee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=6-star-rating-loved-it-rare-epic">6-star-rating-loved-it-rare-epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer638430540" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3358487507487875005"><b>** A spoiler free review** </b><br/><br/><b>** 6 Dangerously Sexy <i>Killer</i> Stars**</b><br/><br/><b>A <i><u>MUST</u></i> read!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424942i/847475.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>This book really had it <i>all</i>! It was a suspense filled, drama packed, thrilling novel with an edge of hot romance. It had my stomach in knots and I was on the edge of my seat from the very beginning. Each sentence was so well put together, the words just rolled off the page like silk. I was completely absorbed in the story, the characters and found myself hanging onto each word like it was my lifeline. I deliberately took </span>
  <span id="freeText3358487507487875005" style="display:none"><b>** A spoiler free review** </b><br><br><b>** 6 Dangerously Sexy <i>Killer</i> Stars**</b><br><br><b>A <i><u>MUST</u></i> read!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424942i/847475.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>This book really had it <i>all</i>! It was a suspense filled, drama packed, thrilling novel with an edge of hot romance. It had my stomach in knots and I was on the edge of my seat from the very beginning. Each sentence was so well put together, the words just rolled off the page like silk. I was completely absorbed in the story, the characters and found myself hanging onto each word like it was my lifeline. I deliberately took my time reading it because I didnt want it to end - <i>it was brillant! </i><br> <br><br>This story is about a girl who tries to escape a life of abuse, murder and salvery. The only way she can escape is to trust a cold-blooded murderer whom she knows nothing about other than he is very dangerous. <br><br><i>Will he help her? <br><br>Will he risk his own life for her? <br><br><b>Or <br><br>Will he kill her?</b></i><br> <br><br><b>
  <u>Sarai</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424942i/847476.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>Sarai</u> was not your typical herione. It was refreshing to see a female lead that was strong and brave. It's expected, that if a person has had to endure so much and suffer from horrific events, to be broken, scarred for life and discover they have become only a shell of a person. Sarai was <i>not</i> one of those people. She was determined, strong and reluctantly learnt how to adjust to dangerous situations by blocking out her fears and emotions. Overtime, she learnt how conceal her hurt and pride by putting up a convincing facade in life threatening situations for the sake of survival. Her character was both admirable and inspiring. However, everything comes at a price ...<br><br><i>Can she change who she has become and live a normal life?</i><br><br><b>Or<br><br>Is she <i>at the point of no return?</i></b><br> <br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm free of a life not of my choosing, because of Victor".~ Sarai </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Victor</u>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424942i/847477._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"We sit in stillness, both looking out ahead, both married to our thoughts. I wonder if hers are about me." ~ Victor </b>
</i><br><br><br><u>Victor</u> is a trained killer. When assigned a hit he fulfills it with no remorse. Life has taught him to trust no one and he won't think twice about ending a persons life. What about the innocent you ask? He believes <i>no one </i> is truly innocent. He <i>trusts</i> no one. Not only he is an assassin but he is also rich, mysterious and attractive - a <i>very</i> dangerous combination.<br><br><br>The relationship between Sarai is slow building which makes it all the more realistic. Alternating POV's between the two characters adds diversity and intrigue to the book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424942i/847478.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b> "I want her to look upon me, just for a moment. But she never does and I walk away". </b>
</i><br><br><br><i>Now</i> the question you all have on your mind....<br><br><b>Is there a cliffhanger?</b><br><br>Well - I will say this. I don't do cliffhangers .. <i>at all</i>. I have, as KC diagnosed it- a <i>cliffhanger disorder</i>. BUT I'm ok..For now anyway! It wasn't as bad as I thought it would be. Yes - there's still a lot of unanswered questions and it's not how I <i>really</i> wanted it to end but ....*takes a deep breath*.. I'm ok, and if <i> I'm </i> ok , you will be fine. It doesn't end with all hearts and flowers but there's potential. Trust me - you will be fine! <br><br>In saying that.....I <b>cannot</b> wait for <i>
  <b>Reviving Izabel!!!!!</b>
</i></span>

<div id="review_1075802859" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1075802859" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1075802859?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=captivity">captivity</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1075802859" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8451718155236370468"><b>2.75 Stars</b><br/><br/>I felt like this wanted to be gritty...but not <i>too</i> gritty.<br/>Sarai was supposed to be innocent/jaded..but not <i>too</i> innocent/jaded.<br/>Victor was supposed to be all cold killer dude...but not <i>too</i> cold.<br/><br/>Get the theme?<br/><br/>I felt like everything was done in half measures. Like the author wanted to be "edgy," but only the <i>politically correct</i> version of edgy. <br/><br/>So instead of actually <i>being</i> edgy, most aspects just came across as trite.<br/><br/>Overall, I thought it was decent...and I'll eventually read the next one.</span>
  <span id="freeText8451718155236370468" style="display:none"><b>2.75 Stars</b><br><br>I felt like this wanted to be gritty...but not <i>too</i> gritty.<br>Sarai was supposed to be innocent/jaded..but not <i>too</i> innocent/jaded.<br>Victor was supposed to be all cold killer dude...but not <i>too</i> cold.<br><br>Get the theme?<br><br>I felt like everything was done in half measures. Like the author wanted to be "edgy," but only the <i>politically correct</i> version of edgy. <br><br>So instead of actually <i>being</i> edgy, most aspects just came across as trite.<br><br>Overall, I thought it was decent...and I'll eventually read the next one...someday (notice the lack of urgency); however, I thought it would have been better if the author had written this story without hesitation - balls to the wall - really gone all the way...bowled without the gutter bumpers if you will.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414593779i/11669197.gif" width="500" height="333" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="8451718155236370468" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Just Wow.<br><br>Words that come to mind after reading this fantastic little book – Suspense. Drama. Action. Sex. Tension. <br><br>I f*cking loved it!!!<br><br>Killing Sarai revolves around the heroine, Sarai. She has been held captive under a disgusting Mexican drug lord for 9 years, living on his compound, and has been his favorite ever since she arrived and has not been able to escape.<br><br>One fateful night, “The American” aka Victor aka Bad Ass MotherF*cker, comes to the compound to discuss a deal with Javier, the drug lord who is holding Sarai captive. Though she knows just by watching that Victor isn’t one to cross and is completely lethal, she sneaks into his car, holds him at gunpoint, and demands he help her.<br><br>Victor, who has been an assassin since he was THIRTEEN (!!!!) is number 1 in “The Order” and has never failed an assignment before. Though after meeting Sarai, he breaks all the rules he has ever known and finds himself fighting against his own thoughts with this insane need to protect her.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I glance over to see her eyes and right now all I see is Sarai looking back at me, the brave but anxious and complicated girl that I’ve grown very protective of.”</i>
</b><br><br>Craziness of course ensues, and a whole bunch of other characters are introduced while the crazy story starts to unfold. I don’t really want to go into that much plot detail. This is one of those books you should go into not knowing too much and just let your mind be blown.<br><br>But I loved everything about this book! The action, the suspense, Sarai who was broken but SO strong, and Victor who was so strong but finds himself bending for Sarai. Even though there wasn’t much “romance” per se, the sexual tension was NOT LACKING.<br><br> I fell in love with the way Victor and Sarai connected with one another. But there was something about this story that grabbed me from the start and DID NOT LET GO.<br><br><b>
  <i>“…while peering into my eyes, though beyond them. I wonder what he’s looking for in their depths. Whatever it is, I hope he never finds it so that we can stay like this forever.”</i>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer645588589" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1215940427965561332"><b>
  <i>“This goes against everything that I am, Sarai,” he says and then kisses me.<br/>“No, it doesn’t,” I whisper and kiss him back.“It’s you becoming more of who you really are.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/sweetjesus_zps37c650e1.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425988ra/850643.gif' alt=' photo sweetjesus_zps37c650e1.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> J.A Redmerski ..</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/bowdown_zps319f4c81.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425988ra/850644.gif' alt=' photo bowdown_zps319f4c81.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Holy fuckin shit .... <br/><br/><b>HOLY.FUCKIN.SHIT !!!!! </b><br/><br/>The ending ... Off the charts amazing ! <br/><br/><a href='http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/creepyassgrin_zpsdb6a808a.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425988ra/850645.gif' alt=' photo creepyassgrin_zpsdb6a808a.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Killing Sarai is the story of Sarai , who has been living as a slave to a Mexican mafia/druglord named Javier for the past 9 years of her life . Javier has a twisted description of the entire scenario though . See</span>
  <span id="freeText1215940427965561332" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“This goes against everything that I am, Sarai,” he says and then kisses me.<br>“No, it doesn’t,” I whisper and kiss him back.“It’s you becoming more of who you really are.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/sweetjesus_zps37c650e1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425988ra/850643.gif" alt=" photo sweetjesus_zps37c650e1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> J.A Redmerski ..</b><br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/bowdown_zps319f4c81.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425988ra/850644.gif" alt=" photo bowdown_zps319f4c81.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Holy fuckin shit .... <br><br><b>HOLY.FUCKIN.SHIT !!!!! </b><br><br>The ending ... Off the charts amazing ! <br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/creepyassgrin_zpsdb6a808a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425988ra/850645.gif" alt=" photo creepyassgrin_zpsdb6a808a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Killing Sarai is the story of Sarai , who has been living as a slave to a Mexican mafia/druglord named Javier for the past 9 years of her life . Javier has a twisted description of the entire scenario though . See , he believes that he is in love with Sarai , a love that is downright obsession . And that's why keeps her locked up in his compound . He basically deals with drugs , weapons and women , so Sarai isn't the only girl in his business and his house . But Sarai wants an escape .. a way out from this hellish life . That escape comes in the form of an American assassin , Victor . Sarai takes her chance and finds a way out of her life in captivity . But her freedom plans are busted when she realizes that she just walked out of hell's circus and ran straight into a lion's den . Victor is a million times dangerous than Javier .. and he has his own plans for Sarai .. What are those plans ? Who is Victor ? What led Sarai to Javier ? And will she ever find a way out of her ordeals ?? To answer those questions you'll just have to be a part of Killing Sarai ! <br><br>You know what the best part about reading this book was ??? It was its unpredictability ! You read that blurb and think , ' hmmm , I might have a clue what's gonna happen here ' and start making your assumptions . But holy damnation !!! You will be in a state of surprise and shock and awe as well with J.A's story weaving skills . I was glued to the pages , and every time I told myself I'll just read one page , I failed miserably in doing so ! The unpredictable twists and turns make it nearly impossible to stop reading and take a breather ! Hell , I stayed up late at night to try and finish but forced myself to stop reading because lets face it , no woman is a fan of watching herself in the mirror and finding huge dark circles and baggy eyes due to lack of sleep . Hell no !<br><br>Another thing that I've noticed about J.A writing <i>( I've read only two books by her so far including Killing Sarai )</i> is that even though she has some really hot , like fan-yo-self-hot moments in her story , she doesn't let the sex/steam moments rule the story line/plot ... That being said , she can write some really hot scenes ! Especially when a guy like Victor is involved !!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/megusta_zps17925479.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425988ra/850646.gif" alt=" photo megusta_zps17925479.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Speaking of the man himself , Victor has to be one of the hottest book boyfriends with the coldest demeanor ever ! He may be hot as hell , but his heart resembles a rock that has been frozen for ages ! No remorse , no regrets ... He is silently lethal ! Victor has his own reasons for being what or who he is .. But that changes when he meets Sarai . <br><br>Sarai on the other hand is one of those leading ladies that can kick some major ass ! Nine years in captivity , witnessing numerous acts of abuse , her defense mechanism technique to cope with all the cruelty around her has enabled her to bottle up all her emotions ! Just the tiniest bit of a shake and she is ready to erupt ! Getting to know Sarai was like unraveling a gift ! Holy hell the things that girl is capable of doing just makes my jaw hit the floor ! Soo did not see those coming ! <br><br>On the whole , Killing Sarai is an addictive fast paced thriller that will keep you on the edge of your seats and your eyes glued to your kindle ! Cannot wait to read Reviving Izabel ... Things are about to get a whole lot more interesting !!! <br><br><b>
  <i> But you did something else that no one else ever could.” His features soften and my heart is slowly melting. “You made me feel real emotions. You unlocked me.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Ozone74/media/VictorandSarai_zps97ddd1cc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425988i/850647.jpg" alt=" photo VictorandSarai_zps97ddd1cc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>

<div id="review_652936271" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/652936271" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/652936271?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer652936271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8119339207408552578"><br/>I have to say, I was a little nervous picking up Killing Sarai because I’ve read dark stories and I didn’t know if my heart could take it. It was dark, but thankfully not on the level I was worried over. Sarai was a heroine that took an opportunity and ran, and I was rooting for her the whole way!<br/><br/>Sarai was taken from the US by her mother at age fourteen to go live with a drug lord, Javier, in Mexico. Unfortunately for Sarai, Javier always had his eye out for her: <br/><b>
  <i><br/>“I call it a sickening obsess</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText8119339207408552578" style="display:none"><br />I have to say, I was a little nervous picking up Killing Sarai because I’ve read dark stories and I didn’t know if my heart could take it. It was dark, but thankfully not on the level I was worried over. Sarai was a heroine that took an opportunity and ran, and I was rooting for her the whole way!<br /><br />Sarai was taken from the US by her mother at age fourteen to go live with a drug lord, Javier, in Mexico. Unfortunately for Sarai, Javier always had his eye out for her: <br /><b>
  <i><br />“I call it a sickening obsession, he calls it love.” -Sarai</i>
</b><br /><br />For the last nine years she’s been his captive, but when an American assassin, Victor, shows up, Sarai sees this as her ticket out of the compound and stows away, thinking he will help her escape back to the US. What she doesn’t realize is that Victor has a cold heart, and helping her is not at the top of his list. Victor is calculating and dangerous!! What Victor doesn’t realize is how much this girl will get under his skin, because it’s a slow undoing for him. Let’s just say, resistance is futile. He sees a fearless, kindred spirit in her. Sarai has been molded by her dark past, just as Victor has by his. This is the best kind of romance, built slowly, but surely! It was a thrill to read the slow progression and growing attraction. <br /><b>
  <i><br />We are one in the same and I don’t want to imagine being on my own without him. Ever.</i>
</b><br /><br />Oh, I was on the edge of my seat for most of this story! If I could’ve, I would’ve read this straight through in one sitting. I was so invested in Sarai and her story of escape and survival! Javier is not about to let her go so easily and I was biting my nails wondering what would happen next! I was impressed with Sarai and her ability to stay strong and unbroken in the face of so much. <br /><br />Victor is an intense, complicated, and determined man, so I couldn't wait to discover the chinks in his armor. We discover that Sarai isn’t his only undoing, but recent events have caused him to question his path in life, as well. <br /><br />J.A. Redmerski managed to write a thrilling mix of suspense, danger with a forbidden romance thrown in. In other words, everything I love in a story! This doesn’t leave off on a cliffhanger, but I’m still desperate for book two!<br /><br />You can read this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2013/07/review-killing-sarai-in-company-of.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8119339207408552578" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_637977282" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637977282" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637977282?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18052619-killing-sarai">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637977282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12653691025288691812">This is a story about two people that were denied a normal childhood and had to change themselves in order to survive. Sarai was given to Javier, a Mexican drug lord, <i> by her drug addict mother (!!)</i>, at the age of fourteen and held hostage for nine years. Victor was recruited by The Order at the age of nine and trained to be an assassin, that's right...an assassin. This is their story. <br/><br/>Okay, so let me just start with a couple of things...the first being this book really has a strong Dark Duet vi</span>
  <span id="freeText12653691025288691812" style="display:none">This is a story about two people that were denied a normal childhood and had to change themselves in order to survive. Sarai was given to Javier, a Mexican drug lord, <i> by her drug addict mother (!!)</i>, at the age of fourteen and held hostage for nine years. Victor was recruited by The Order at the age of nine and trained to be an assassin, that's right...an assassin. This is their story. <br><br>Okay, so let me just start with a couple of things...the first being this book really has a strong Dark Duet vibe for me. Not the same intensity but definitely the same feel. Second, when the book was first put up with no blurb, the title alone was a little scary. And there's good reason...it <b>IS</b> about killing, lots of killing and lots of blood. Yes, there's some romance but it's definitely not your usual romance. Lastly, there's not <i>really</i> a cliffhanger...not in the sense of <b>OMG, WHAT IN THE EFF IS HAPPENING</b>!! No, not like that but maybe...<i>omg, what in the heck is happening</i>! It does end unfinished and that's why there's book two! (Can't wait for <i>Reviving Izabel</i>!!)<br><br>So Caleb, err I mean Victor ;)...is cool, calm and collective. He's a man of many faces. The story is told in alternating POVs so thank goodness we get his thoughts. I'm not sure I would've liked it as much if we hadn't. And...it takes a while to get to know him and what he is thinking but it makes the journey very intriguing.<br><br><u><b>Victor</b> (but with shorter hair!)</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582142._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sarai was amazing...definitely a survivor but she has somehow managed to keep her kind heart...and I like to think that's what Victor sees. She's been traumatized but somehow she focuses that into what she needs to do and it's made her stronger. And her feelings for Victor are a little befuddled. Yes, he helped her and yes, she has no one else but is that why she is developing feelings for him? <br><br>The 'romance' was killing me. Like I said, this is not a typical romance but you know there's so much potential. The frustrating part is we only find out things s-l-o-w-l-y and we're never really sure what is real as far as what Victor and Sarai are feeling. Well, maybe Sarai....and I want to think Victor too but you have to read it and see. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/584335.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, of course, there's lots of drama...betrayals and blindsides. It definitely keeps things interesting. There's also some crazy characters...namely Niklas, Victor's brother. I'm not a fan of his but I do agree with what Sarai did towards the end. <br><br>The "ending"...made me a little sad. I was hoping for a little more breakthrough but there is...possibility and that's always promising. I was happy with how Victor set things up for Sarai and I loved the surprise person! ~sigh~ <br><br>I would definitely recommend reading this if you want something a little dark, a little different and something you cannot put down. ♥ <b>Thank you, Chiqui</b>, for pushing me to read it and letting me have one of "your men" for a short time! ♥ <br><br><b>♦ Bonus!! ♦ </b> We get an excerpt for <i>The Edge of Always</i> at the end and while it's really good, I can't believe she left it like that....ugh!! <br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4Tr0otuiQuU" rel="nofollow noopener">♥ Victor and Sarai's song ♥</a><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/597121.gif" width="400" height="025" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Favorite quotes: <b>(Beware they may have minor spoilers)</b><br><br>♦ <i>“I knew you had it in you, Sarai.”</i> (that haunts me!)<br><br>♥ “I don’t want to sleep alone,” she says gently. <br><br>And I don’t force her to. Sarai falls fast asleep curled up next to me in my bed. Right where I want her." <i>(~sigh~)</i><br><br>♦ " smothering me like way too much jelly on a PB&amp;J." <i>(partial quote but the image is sooo gross...I can't get it out of my head!!)</i><br><br>♥ “But you did something else that no one else ever could.” His features soften and my heart is slowly melting. “You made me feel real emotions. You unlocked me.” <i>(thud!)</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12653691025288691812" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer13942210684026660470">If you haven't read Killing Sarai yet, you are missing out. This was everything I was hoping it would be and so much more. I was seriously trying to catch my breath while reading. I could kick myself for waiting so long to read this. <br/><br/>Victor<br/><a href='http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/EDF23305-A1FF-4D69-B3AD-9D3FD07349A9_zpsfsytvohp.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463176478i/19090383._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo EDF23305-A1FF-4D69-B3AD-9D3FD07349A9_zpsfsytvohp.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Victor is disciplined, in control and a ruthless killer. He is part of a " secret organization". He kills for money and he is damned good at it. Nothing gets in his way... Ever!! <br/><br/>Sarai <br/><a href='http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/911DD6B9-B457-486B-A579-04DEBDDC2C0B_zpsdapxctxq.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463176478i/19090384._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 911DD6B9-B457-486B-A579-04DEBDDC2C0B_zpsdapxctxq.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Sarai was taken to Mexico when she was 14 and held captive for 9 ye</span>
  <span id="freeText13942210684026660470" style="display:none">If you haven't read Killing Sarai yet, you are missing out. This was everything I was hoping it would be and so much more. I was seriously trying to catch my breath while reading. I could kick myself for waiting so long to read this. <br><br>Victor<br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/EDF23305-A1FF-4D69-B3AD-9D3FD07349A9_zpsfsytvohp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463176478i/19090383._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo EDF23305-A1FF-4D69-B3AD-9D3FD07349A9_zpsfsytvohp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Victor is disciplined, in control and a ruthless killer. He is part of a " secret organization". He kills for money and he is damned good at it. Nothing gets in his way... Ever!! <br><br>Sarai <br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/911DD6B9-B457-486B-A579-04DEBDDC2C0B_zpsdapxctxq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Sarai was taken to Mexico when she was 14 and held captive for 9 years. She has witnessed drugs, rapes and murders, all while living in this compound with one of the most vicious dealers in Mexico. She is Javier's " favorite" but she still tries desperately to get free. <br><br>She hears Javier talking to an American man and decides to make a run for it and jumps in the Americans car. That is when she meets Victor. He has no idea what to do with her and can't kick her out because she has a gun to his head. From there they are on the run.<br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/938683DB-6885-4F24-83BB-A5926B3B8B3D_zpswvoyrwvq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Sarai was the perfect heroine and Victor, though vicious he was the perfect hero. <br><br>I think what I liked the most about Victor was his control. He never shows emotions and it works for him. I instantly liked him...ALOT!! <br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/450CCE9B-B4D6-4D14-AE5A-3F3E6EB63B59_zpsf6rgn1fp.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463176478ra/19090386.gif" alt=" photo 450CCE9B-B4D6-4D14-AE5A-3F3E6EB63B59_zpsf6rgn1fp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sarai is broken and full of rage but I am hoping as time goes on she will heal and hopefully live a nice and calm life. She deserves it because she has been through so much. <br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/2EC7ED98-6A28-475A-A09A-D5303B212F08_zpshswmfojp.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>As far as Victor is concerned, I can't wait to see who his next kill is.<br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/98B2B2C0-77F2-49C4-BC55-127FE75EBD44_zpsrafgtutg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I am running to book two like... <br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/9138F2F5-AD52-46A2-9C67-C70E34452C3A_zpsntdhkh4p.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer642800448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4713932732318310690"><b>Reread October 2017</b><br/>- Rereading before <i>Spiders in the Grove</i> releases. I made my guesses of who's going to betray on book 7th and I don't like my guesses at all. It makes me nervous.😩 Anyways, I miss my favorite group of assassins and I enjoyed this book for the second time. I'm still rooting for Victor & Izabel peeps ;) <br/><br/>-------------------------------------------<br/><b>First read: January 2016</b><br/><br/>This is one of the cases when you are trying to come up with words but couldn't think of any. I had a hard time </span>
  <span id="freeText4713932732318310690" style="display:none"><b>Reread October 2017</b><br />- Rereading before <i>Spiders in the Grove</i> releases. I made my guesses of who's going to betray on book 7th and I don't like my guesses at all. It makes me nervous.😩 Anyways, I miss my favorite group of assassins and I enjoyed this book for the second time. I'm still rooting for Victor &amp; Izabel peeps ;) <br /><br />-------------------------------------------<br /><b>First read: January 2016</b><br /><br />This is one of the cases when you are trying to come up with words but couldn't think of any. I had a hard time organizing my thoughts. <b>I am absolutely stunned and speechless. </b> J.A. Redmerski indeed surprised me. I am beyond impressed she pulled off something darker and more twisted story than <i>The Edge of Never</i> and <i>The Edge of Always</i>, which are my favorites.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"She's already so anesthetized to what is normal that she might never live a normal life."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />The story is about a twenty three year old girl named Sarai. Her mother let a Mexican drug lord to have her at fourteen years old. For years, she didn't have a normal life and somewhat got used to witness death and violence. When she overheard a conversation between Javier and the American, that became an opportunity to escape. What she didn't know that Victor - the American- is a dangerous, merciless assassin on mission. She took the risk of getting in his car, maybe he can help her and is on the run..<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I am discipline. Sarai is rage."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Victor didn't really offer to help Sarai but he lets her to go with him and thinks of a strategy on how she will be useful during his job. Everything is unplanned and he needs to come up with a new strategy to get it done. Being an assassin, he does not allow himself to be emotionally attached to someone. However, there is something about the girl that makes him want to protect her from danger. He wants her to give a shot of a normal life she truly deserved. Doing so, he is risking his life for it.<br /><br />I will not tell you much about it because there are so many things happened. I am fully engrossed with the story. It is <b>thrilling, intense, action-packed,and mind-blowing.</b> It's better that you get into it without knowing too much and let the surprises take over. <b>Every chapter is heart pounding and will definitely put you on the edge of your seat. </b> The sequence of events are well written. The plot twists are so good, I swear. REALLY GOOD. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You made me feel real emotions. You unlocked me."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><b>Sarai and Victor are fascinating and strong-willed characters.</b> I am so amused and hooked with these two. Sarai isn't bothered of Victor being an assassin. She tried engaging him with conversations and is very patient with it. He's the only one whom she can trust with. What they have been through made them closer. <b>The characters are well developed and had a wonderful intensified romantic build up</b> <br /><br />Without any doubt, this series deserves a rave. I think I made a good decision to finally read it because I'm going to read the sequel ASAP. This cliffhanger makes me want to read more and I crave for it. I just splurge everything here. <br /><br />Thank you <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639306505" rel="nofollow noopener">Sylvia</a> (click to read her review) for recommending this book to me. There is an <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/180025-in-the-company-of-killers-readalong" rel="nofollow noopener">"In the Company of Killers" Read-a-long</a> hosted by Riley and Lainey (which I'm participating. Thank you for hosting! Now, I'm gonna read <i>Reviving Izabel</i>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4713932732318310690" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }

      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");

      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }

    }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1598797459718270265">J.A. (Jessica) Redmerski is a <i>New York Times</i>, <i>USA Today,</i> and <i>Wall Street Journal</i> bestselling author, international bestseller, and award winner, who juggles several different genres. She began self-publishing in 2012, and later with the success of THE EDGE OF NEVER, signed on with Grand Central Publishing/Forever Romance. Her works have been translated into more than twenty languages.<br/><br/>Jessica is a </span>
  <span id="freeText1598797459718270265" style="display:none">J.A. (Jessica) Redmerski is a <i>New York Times</i>, <i>USA Today,</i> and <i>Wall Street Journal</i> bestselling author, international bestseller, and award winner, who juggles several different genres. She began self-publishing in 2012, and later with the success of THE EDGE OF NEVER, signed on with Grand Central Publishing/Forever Romance. Her works have been translated into more than twenty languages.<br /><br />Jessica is a hybrid author who, in addition to working with a traditional publisher, also continues to self-publish. Her popular crime and suspense series, <i>In the Company of Killers</i>, has been optioned for television and film by actor and model William Levy.<br /><br />What book is Jessica most proud to have written? It's a question she gets asked often. The answer is, hands down, DIRTY EDEN. <i>"DIRTY EDEN was an entirely organic experience for me, as was the story from beginning to end; nothing was planned, and I didn't know the end myself until I got there. As much as I enjoy writing love stories and crime novels, a big part of my heart really does lie in the satirical and strange. I just wish more people would read it."</i><br /><br />What book is Jessica most proud to have written? It's a question she gets asked quite often. The answer is, hands down, DIRTY EDEN. <i>"DIRTY EDEN was an entirely organic experience for me, as was the story from beginning to end; nothing was planned, and I didn't know the end myself until I got there. As much as I enjoy writing love stories and crime novels, a big part of my heart really does lie in the satirical and strange. I just wish more people would read it."</i></span>
